          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 " style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 36px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:4646198,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes-litecoin.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e1d650917cd5c3ba8befb5c90d11b4b726d2c80b9107acffeafb7274e66fbd51" href="#gui">GUI</a>
          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 " style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 36px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:4646198,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes-litecoin.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e1d650917cd5c3ba8befb5c90d11b4b726d2c80b9107acffeafb7274e66fbd51" href="#build-system">Build system</a>
          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 " style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 36px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:4646198,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes-litecoin.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e1d650917cd5c3ba8befb5c90d11b4b726d2c80b9107acffeafb7274e66fbd51" href="#tests-and-qa">Tests and QA</a>
          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 " style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 36px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:4646198,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes-litecoin.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e1d650917cd5c3ba8befb5c90d11b4b726d2c80b9107acffeafb7274e66fbd51" href="#platform-support">Platform support</a>
          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 " style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 36px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:4646198,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes-litecoin.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e1d650917cd5c3ba8befb5c90d11b4b726d2c80b9107acffeafb7274e66fbd51" href="#miscellaneous">Miscellaneous</a>
          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 " style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 36px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:4646198,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes-litecoin.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e1d650917cd5c3ba8befb5c90d11b4b726d2c80b9107acffeafb7274e66fbd51" href="#documentation-1">Documentation</a>
          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 text-emphasized" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 12px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:4646198,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes-litecoin.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e1d650917cd5c3ba8befb5c90d11b4b726d2c80b9107acffeafb7274e66fbd51" href="#credits">Credits</a>

        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><p dir="auto">Litecoin Core version 0.18.1 is now available from:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://download.litecoin.org/litecoin-0.18.1/" rel="nofollow">https://download.litecoin.org/litecoin-0.18.1/</a></p>
<p dir="auto">This is a major version release, including new features, various bug
fixes and performance improvements, as well as updated translations.</p>
<p dir="auto">Please report bugs using the issue tracker at GitHub:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/issues">https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/issues</a></p>
<p dir="auto">To receive security and update notifications, please subscribe to:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://groups.google.com/forum/#!forum/litecoin-dev" rel="nofollow">https://groups.google.com/forum/#!forum/litecoin-dev</a></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-to-upgrade" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-upgrade"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>How to Upgrade</h1>
<p dir="auto">If you are running an older version, shut it down. Wait until it has
completely shut down (which might take a few minutes for older
versions), then run the installer (on Windows) or just copy over
<code>/Applications/Litecoin-Qt</code> (on Mac) or <code>litecoind</code>/<code>litecoin-qt</code> (on
Linux).</p>
<p dir="auto">The first time you run version 0.15.0 or newer, your chainstate database
will be converted to a new format, which will take anywhere from a few
minutes to half an hour, depending on the speed of your machine.</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that the block database format also changed in version 0.8.0 and
there is no automatic upgrade code from before version 0.8 to version
0.15.0 or later. Upgrading directly from 0.7.x and earlier without
redownloading the blockchain is not supported.  However, as usual, old
wallet versions are still supported.</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-compatibility" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#compatibility"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Compatibility</h1>
<p dir="auto">Litecoin Core is supported and extensively tested on operating systems
using the Linux kernel, macOS 10.10+, and Windows 7 and newer. It is not
recommended to use Litecoin Core on unsupported systems.</p>
<p dir="auto">Litecoin Core should also work on most other Unix-like systems but is not
as frequently tested on them.</p>
<p dir="auto">From 0.17.0 onwards, macOS &lt;10.10 is no longer supported. 0.17.0 is
built using Qt 5.9.x, which doesn't support versions of macOS older than
10.10. Additionally, Litecoin Core does not yet change appearance when
macOS "dark mode" is activated.</p>
<p dir="auto">In addition to previously-supported CPU platforms, this release's
pre-compiled distribution also provides binaries for the RISC-V
platform.</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-known-issues" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#known-issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Known issues</h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-wallet-gui" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#wallet-gui"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Wallet GUI</h2>
<p dir="auto">For advanced users who have both (1) enabled coin control features, and
(2) are using multiple wallets loaded at the same time: The coin control
input selection dialog can erroneously retain wrong-wallet state when
switching wallets using the dropdown menu. For now, it is recommended
not to use coin control features with multiple wallets loaded.</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-notable-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#notable-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Notable changes</h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-mining" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mining"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Mining</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Calls to <code>getblocktemplate</code> will fail if the segwit rule is not
specified.  Calling <code>getblocktemplate</code> without segwit specified is
almost certainly a misconfiguration since doing so results in lower
rewards for the miner.  Failed calls will produce an error message
describing how to enable the segwit rule.</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-configuration-option-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#configuration-option-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Configuration option changes</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">A warning is printed if an unrecognized section name is used in the
configuration file.  Recognized sections are <code>[test]</code>, <code>[main]</code>, and
<code>[regtest]</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Four new options are available for configuring the maximum number of
messages that ZMQ will queue in memory (the "high water mark") before
dropping additional messages.  The default value is 1,000, the same as
was used for previous releases.  See the <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/zmq.md#usage">ZMQ
documentation</a>
for details.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>rpcallowip</code> option can no longer be used to automatically listen
on all network interfaces.  Instead, the <code>rpcbind</code> parameter must be
used to specify the IP addresses to listen on.  Listening for RPC
commands over a public network connection is insecure and should be
disabled, so a warning is now printed if a user selects such a
configuration.  If you need to expose RPC in order to use a tool like
Docker, ensure you only bind RPC to your localhost, e.g. <code>docker run [...] -p 127.0.0.1:9332:9332</code> (this is an extra <code>:9332</code> over the
normal Docker port specification).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>rpcpassword</code> option now causes a startup error if the password
set in the configuration file contains a hash character (#), as it's
ambiguous whether the hash character is meant for the password or as a
comment.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>whitelistforcerelay</code> option is used to relay transactions from
whitelisted peers even when not accepted to the mempool. This option
now defaults to being off, so that changes in policy and
disconnect/ban behavior will not cause a node that is whitelisting
another to be dropped by peers.  Users can still explicitly enable
this behavior with the command line option (and may want to consider
<a href="mailto:contact@litecoin.org">contacting</a> the Litecoin Core
project to let us know about their use-case, as this feature could be
deprecated in the future).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-wallet-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#wallet-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Wallet changes</h2>
<p dir="auto">When creating a transaction with a fee above <code>-maxtxfee</code> (default 0.1 LTC),
the RPC commands <code>walletcreatefundedpsbt</code> and  <code>fundrawtransaction</code> will now fail
instead of rounding down the fee. Beware that the <code>feeRate</code> argument is specified
in LTC per kilobyte, not litoshi per byte.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-documentation" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Documentation</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">A new short <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/JSON-RPC-interface.md">document</a>
about the JSON-RPC interface describes cases where the results of an
RPC might contain inconsistencies between data sourced from different
subsystems, such as wallet state and mempool state.  A note is added
to the <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/REST-interface.md">REST interface documentation</a>
indicating that the same rules apply.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Further information is added to the <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/JSON-RPC-interface.md">JSON-RPC
documentation</a>
about how to secure this interface.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A new <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/litecoin-conf.md">document</a>
about the <code>litecoin.conf</code> file describes how to use it to configure
Litecoin Core.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A new document introduces Litecoin Core's BIP174 <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/psbt.md">Partially-Signed
Litecoin Transactions
(PSBT)</a>
interface, which is used to allow multiple programs to collaboratively
work to create, sign, and broadcast new transactions.  This is useful
for offline (cold storage) wallets, multisig wallets, coinjoin
implementations, and many other cases where two or more programs need
to interact to generate a complete transaction.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/descriptors.md">output script
descriptor</a>
documentation has been updated with information about new features in
this still-developing language for describing the output scripts that
a wallet or other program wants to receive notifications for, such as
which addresses it wants to know received payments.  The language is
currently used in multiple new and updated RPCs described in these
release notes and is expected to be adapted to other RPCs and to the
underlying wallet structure.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-build-system-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#build-system-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Build system changes</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">A new <code>--disable-bip70</code> option may be passed to <code>./configure</code> to
prevent Litecoin-Qt from being built with support for the BIP70 payment
protocol or from linking libssl.  As the payment protocol has exposed
Litecoin Core to libssl vulnerabilities in the past, builders who don't
need BIP70 support are encouraged to use this option to reduce their
exposure to future vulnerabilities.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The minimum required version of Qt (when building the GUI) has been
increased from 5.2 to 5.5.1 (the <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/depends/README.md">depends
system</a>
provides 5.9.7)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-new-rpcs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#new-rpcs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>New RPCs</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>getnodeaddresses</code> returns peer addresses known to this node. It may
be used to find nodes to connect to without using a DNS seeder.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>listwalletdir</code> returns a list of wallets in the wallet directory
(either the default wallet directory or the directory configured by
the <code>-walletdir</code> parameter).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>getrpcinfo</code> returns runtime details of the RPC server. At the moment,
it returns an array of the currently active commands and how long
they've been running.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>deriveaddresses</code> returns one or more addresses corresponding to an
<a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/descriptors.md">output descriptor</a>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>getdescriptorinfo</code> accepts a descriptor and returns information about
it, including its computed checksum.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>joinpsbts</code> merges multiple distinct PSBTs into a single PSBT. The
multiple PSBTs must have different inputs. The resulting PSBT will
contain every input and output from all of the PSBTs. Any signatures
provided in any of the PSBTs will be dropped.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>analyzepsbt</code> examines a PSBT and provides information about what
the PSBT contains and the next steps that need to be taken in order
to complete the transaction. For each input of a PSBT, <code>analyzepsbt</code>
provides information about what information is missing for that
input, including whether a UTXO needs to be provided, what pubkeys
still need to be provided, which scripts need to be provided, and
what signatures are still needed. Every input will also list which
role is needed to complete that input, and <code>analyzepsbt</code> will also
list the next role in general needed to complete the PSBT.
<code>analyzepsbt</code> will also provide the estimated fee rate and estimated
virtual size of the completed transaction if it has enough
information to do so.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>utxoupdatepsbt</code> searches the set of Unspent Transaction Outputs
(UTXOs) to find the outputs being spent by the partial transaction.
PSBTs need to have the UTXOs being spent to be provided because
the signing algorithm requires information from the UTXO being spent.
For segwit inputs, only the UTXO itself is necessary.  For
non-segwit outputs, the entire previous transaction is needed so
that signers can be sure that they are signing the correct thing.
Unfortunately, because the UTXO set only contains UTXOs and not full
transactions, <code>utxoupdatepsbt</code> will only add the UTXO for segwit
inputs.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-updated-rpcs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#updated-rpcs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Updated RPCs</h2>
<p dir="auto">Note: some low-level RPC changes mainly useful for testing are described
in the Low-level Changes section below.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>getpeerinfo</code> now returns an additional <code>minfeefilter</code> field set to
the peer's BIP133 fee filter.  You can use this to detect that you
have peers that are willing to accept transactions below the default
minimum relay fee.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The mempool RPCs, such as <code>getrawmempool</code> with <code>verbose=true</code>, now
return an additional "bip125-replaceable" value indicating whether the
transaction (or its unconfirmed ancestors) opts-in to asking nodes and
miners to replace it with a higher-feerate transaction spending any of
the same inputs.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>settxfee</code> previously silently ignored attempts to set the fee below
the allowed minimums.  It now prints a warning.  The special value of
"0" may still be used to request the minimum value.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>getaddressinfo</code> now provides an <code>ischange</code> field indicating whether
the wallet used the address in a change output.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>importmulti</code> has been updated to support P2WSH, P2WPKH, P2SH-P2WPKH,
and P2SH-P2WSH. Requests for P2WSH and P2SH-P2WSH accept an additional
<code>witnessscript</code> parameter.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>importmulti</code> now returns an additional <code>warnings</code> field for each
request with an array of strings explaining when fields are being
ignored or are inconsistent, if there are any.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>getaddressinfo</code> now returns an additional <code>solvable</code> boolean field
when Litecoin Core knows enough about the address's scriptPubKey,
optional redeemScript, and optional witnessScript in order for the
wallet to be able to generate an unsigned input spending funds sent to
that address.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>getaddressinfo</code>, <code>listunspent</code>, and <code>scantxoutset</code> RPCs now
return an additional <code>desc</code> field that contains an output descriptor
containing all key paths and signing information for the address
(except for the private key).  The <code>desc</code> field is only returned for
<code>getaddressinfo</code> and <code>listunspent</code> when the address is solvable.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>importprivkey</code> will preserve previously-set labels for addresses or
public keys corresponding to the private key being imported.  For
example, if you imported a watch-only address with the label "cold
wallet" in earlier releases of Litecoin Core, subsequently importing
the private key would default to resetting the address's label to the
default empty-string label ("").  In this release, the previous label
of "cold wallet" will be retained.  If you optionally specify any
label besides the default when calling <code>importprivkey</code>, the new label
will be applied to the address.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="#mining">Mining</a> section for changes to <code>getblocktemplate</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>getmininginfo</code> now omits <code>currentblockweight</code> and <code>currentblocktx</code>
when a block was never assembled via RPC on this node.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>getrawtransaction</code> RPC &amp; REST endpoints no longer check the
unspent UTXO set for a transaction. The remaining behaviors are as
follows: 1. If a blockhash is provided, check the corresponding block.
2. If no blockhash is provided, check the mempool. 3. If no blockhash
is provided but txindex is enabled, also check txindex.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>unloadwallet</code> is now synchronous, meaning it will not return until
the wallet is fully unloaded.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>importmulti</code> now supports importing of addresses from descriptors. A
"desc" parameter can be provided instead of the "scriptPubKey" in a
request, as well as an optional range for ranged descriptors to
specify the start and end of the range to import. Descriptors with key
origin information imported through <code>importmulti</code> will have their key
origin information stored in the wallet for use with creating PSBTs.
More information about descriptors can be found
<a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/descriptors.md">here</a>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>listunspent</code> has been modified so that it also returns
<code>witnessScript</code>, the witness script in the case of a P2WSH or
P2SH-P2WSH output.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>createwallet</code> now has an optional <code>blank</code> argument that can be used
to create a blank wallet. Blank wallets do not have any keys or HD
seed.  They cannot be opened in software older than 0.18. Once a blank
wallet has a HD seed set (by using <code>sethdseed</code>) or private keys,
scripts, addresses, and other watch only things have been imported,
the wallet is no longer blank and can be opened in 0.17.x. Encrypting
a blank wallet will also set a HD seed for it.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-deprecated-or-removed-rpcs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#deprecated-or-removed-rpcs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Deprecated or removed RPCs</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>signrawtransaction</code> is removed after being deprecated and hidden
behind a special configuration option in version 0.17.0.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The 'account' API is removed after being deprecated in v0.17.  The
'label' API was introduced in v0.17 as a replacement for accounts.
See the <a href="https://github.com/litecoin-project/litecoin/blob/master/doc/release-notes/release-notes-0.17.0.md#label-and-account-apis-for-wallet">release notes from
v0.17</a>
for a full description of the changes from the 'account' API to the
'label' API.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>addwitnessaddress</code> is removed after being deprecated in version
0.16.0.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>generate</code> is deprecated and will be fully removed in a subsequent
major version.  This RPC is only used for testing, but its
implementation reached across multiple subsystems (wallet and mining),
so it is being deprecated to simplify the wallet-node interface.
Projects that are using <code>generate</code> for testing purposes should
transition to using the <code>generatetoaddress</code> RPC, which does not
require or use the wallet component. Calling <code>generatetoaddress</code> with
an address returned by the <code>getnewaddress</code> RPC gives the same
functionality as the old <code>generate</code> RPC.  To continue using <code>generate</code>
in this version, restart litecoind with the <code>-deprecatedrpc=generate</code>
configuration option.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Be reminded that parts of the <code>validateaddress</code> command have been
deprecated and moved to <code>getaddressinfo</code>. The following deprecated
fields have moved to <code>getaddressinfo</code>: <code>ismine</code>, <code>iswatchonly</code>,
<code>script</code>, <code>hex</code>, <code>pubkeys</code>, <code>sigsrequired</code>, <code>pubkey</code>, <code>embedded</code>,
<code>iscompressed</code>, <code>label</code>, <code>timestamp</code>, <code>hdkeypath</code>, <code>hdmasterkeyid</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>addresses</code> field has been removed from the <code>validateaddress</code>
and <code>getaddressinfo</code> RPC methods.  This field was confusing since
it referred to public keys using their P2PKH address.  Clients
should use the <code>embedded.address</code> field for P2SH or P2WSH wrapped
addresses, and <code>pubkeys</code> for inspecting multisig participants.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-rest-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rest-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>REST changes</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A new <code>/rest/blockhashbyheight/</code> endpoint is added for fetching the
hash of the block in the current best blockchain based on its height
(how many blocks it is after the Genesis Block).</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-graphical-user-interface-gui" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#graphical-user-interface-gui"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Graphical User Interface (GUI)</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">A new Window menu is added alongside the existing File, Settings, and
Help menus.  Several items from the other menus that opened new
windows have been moved to this new Window menu.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">In the Send tab, the checkbox for "pay only the required fee" has been
removed.  Instead, the user can simply decrease the value in the
Custom Feerate field all the way down to the node's configured minimum
relay fee.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">In the Overview tab, the watch-only balance will be the only balance
shown if the wallet was created using the <code>createwallet</code> RPC and the
<code>disable_private_keys</code> parameter was set to true.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The launch-on-startup option is no longer available on macOS if
compiled with macosx min version greater than 10.11 (use
CXXFLAGS="-mmacosx-version-min=10.11"
CFLAGS="-mmacosx-version-min=10.11" for setting the deployment sdk
version)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-tools" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Tools</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A new <code>litecoin-wallet</code> tool is now distributed alongside Litecoin
Core's other executables.  Without needing to use any RPCs, this tool
can currently create a new wallet file or display some basic
information about an existing wallet, such as whether the wallet is
encrypted, whether it uses an HD seed, how many transactions it
contains, and how many address book entries it has.</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-planned-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#planned-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Planned changes</h1>
<p dir="auto">This section describes planned changes to Litecoin Core that may affect
other Litecoin software and services.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Since version 0.16.0, Litecoin Cores built-in wallet has defaulted to
generating P2SH-wrapped segwit addresses when users want to receive
payments. These addresses are backwards compatible with all
widely-used software.  Starting with Litecoin Core 0.20 (expected about
a year after 0.18), Litecoin Core will default to native segwit
addresses (bech32) that provide additional fee savings and other
benefits. Currently, many wallets and services already support sending
to bech32 addresses, and if the Litecoin Core project sees enough
additional adoption, it will instead default to bech32 receiving
addresses in Litecoin Core 0.20.
P2SH-wrapped segwit addresses will continue to be provided if the user
requests them in the GUI or by RPC, and anyone who doesnt want the
update will be able to configure their default address type.
(Similarly, pioneering users who want to change their default now may
set the <code>addresstype=bech32</code> configuration option in any Litecoin Core
release from 0.16.0 up.)</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-deprecated-p2p-messages" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#deprecated-p2p-messages"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Deprecated P2P messages</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>BIP 61 reject messages are now deprecated. Reject messages have no use
case on the P2P network and are only logged for debugging by most
network nodes. Furthermore, they increase bandwidth and can be harmful
for privacy and security. It has been possible to disable BIP 61
messages since v0.17 with the <code>-enablebip61=0</code> option. BIP 61 messages
will be disabled by default in a future version, before being removed
entirely.</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-low-level-changes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#low-level-changes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Low-level changes</h1>
<p dir="auto">This section describes RPC changes mainly useful for testing, mostly not
relevant in production. The changes are mentioned for completeness.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-rpc" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rpc"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>RPC</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>submitblock</code> RPC previously returned the reason a rejected block
was invalid the first time it processed that block, but returned a
generic "duplicate" rejection message on subsequent occasions it
processed the same block.  It now always returns the fundamental
reason for rejecting an invalid block and only returns "duplicate" for
valid blocks it has already accepted.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A new <code>submitheader</code> RPC allows submitting block headers independently
from their block.  This is likely only useful for testing.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The <code>signrawtransactionwithkey</code> and <code>signrawtransactionwithwallet</code>
RPCs have been modified so that they also optionally accept a
<code>witnessScript</code>, the witness script in the case of a P2WSH or
P2SH-P2WSH output. This is compatible with the change to
<code>listunspent</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">For the <code>walletprocesspsbt</code> and <code>walletcreatefundedpsbt</code> RPCs, if the
<code>bip32derivs</code> parameter is set to true but the key metadata for a
public key has not been updated yet, then that key will have a
derivation path as if it were just an independent key (i.e. no
derivation path and its master fingerprint is itself).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-configuration" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Configuration</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The <code>-usehd</code> configuration option was removed in version 0.16. From
that version onwards, all new wallets created are hierarchical
deterministic wallets. This release makes specifying <code>-usehd</code> an
invalid configuration option.</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-network" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#network"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Network</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This release allows peers that your node automatically disconnected
for misbehavior (e.g. sending invalid data) to reconnect to your node
if you have unused incoming connection slots.  If your slots fill up,
a misbehaving node will be disconnected to make room for nodes without
a history of problems (unless the misbehaving node helps your node in
some other way, such as by connecting to a part of the Internet from
which you don't have many other peers).  Previously, Litecoin Core
banned the IP addresses of misbehaving peers for a period of time
(default of 1 day); this was easily circumvented by attackers with
multiple IP addresses. If you manually ban a peer, such as by using
the <code>setban</code> RPC, all connections from that peer will still be
rejected.</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-wallet" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#wallet"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Wallet</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">The key metadata will need to be upgraded the first time that the HD
seed is available.  For unencrypted wallets this will occur on wallet
loading.  For encrypted wallets this will occur the first time the
wallet is unlocked.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Newly encrypted wallets will no longer require restarting the
software. Instead such wallets will be completely unloaded and
reloaded to achieve the same effect.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A sub-project of Litecoin Core now provides Hardware Wallet Interaction
(HWI) scripts that allow command-line users to use several popular
hardware key management devices with Litecoin Core.  See their <a href="https://github.com/bitcoin-core/HWI#readme">project
page</a> for details.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-security" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#security"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Security</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>This release changes the Random Number Generator (RNG) used from
OpenSSL to Litecoin Core's own implementation, although entropy
gathered by Litecoin Core is fed out to OpenSSL and then read back in
when the program needs strong randomness. This moves Litecoin Core a
little closer to no longer needing to depend on OpenSSL, a dependency
that has caused security issues in the past.  The new implementation
gathers entropy from multiple sources, including from hardware
supporting the rdseed CPU instruction.</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-changes-for-particular-platforms" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#changes-for-particular-platforms"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Changes for particular platforms</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>On macOS, Litecoin Core now opts out of application CPU throttling
("app nap") during initial blockchain download, when catching up from
over 100 blocks behind the current chain tip, or when reindexing chain
data. This helps prevent these operations from taking an excessively
long time because the operating system is attempting to conserve
power.</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-0181-change-log" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#0181-change-log"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>0.18.1 change log</h1>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-consensus" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#consensus"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Consensus</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>#14247 Fix crash bug with duplicate inputs within a transaction (TheBlueMatt)</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-mining-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mining-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Mining</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>#14811 Mining: Enforce that segwit option must be set in GBT (jnewbery)</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-block-and-transaction-handling" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#block-and-transaction-handling"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Block and transaction handling</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>#13310 Report progress in ReplayBlocks while rolling forward (promag)</li>
<li>#13783 validation: Pass tx pool reference into CheckSequenceLocks (MarcoFalke)</li>
<li>#14834 validation: Assert that pindexPrev is non-null when required (kallewoof)</li>
<li>#14085 index: Fix for indexers skipping genesis block (jimpo)</li>
<li>#14963 mempool, validation: Explain <code>cs_main</code> locking semantics (MarcoFalke)</li>
<li>#15193 Default <code>-whitelistforcerelay</code> to off (sdaftuar)</li>
<li>#15429 Update <code>assumevalid</code>, <code>minimumchainwork</code>, and <code>getchaintxstats</code> to height 563378 (gmaxwell)</li>
<li>#15552 Granular invalidateblock and RewindBlockIndex (MarcoFalke)</li>
<li>#14841 Move CheckBlock() call to critical section (hebasto)</li>
</ul>
